            var $wildCatTable = $wildCat.find('.catalog_main_table');
            var $wildCatContent = $wildCat.find('#catalog-content');
            if ($wildCatTable.length !== 0) {
                var catParams = $wildCatContent.data('catalog-params');
                if (catParams && !catParams.sle && catParams.page === 1)
                        resultsCount = catParams.totalItems;
            }
        }

        sendSearchStatistics(resultsCount);
    

});

        if (!wb.settings.isMobileDevice && !wb.settings.disableBackground) {
            var $leftBg = $('.left-bg'),
                $body = $('.main-content'),
                leftBackground = '',
                rightBackground = '',
                backgroundColor = '';
            
            if (leftBackground)
                $leftBg.css('background', leftBackground);
            if (rightBackground)
                $body.css('background', rightBackground);
            if (backgroundColor)
                $leftBg.css('background-color', backgroundColor);
        }
    

    
            (function () {
                $.when(wb.utils.script.require('//static.wbstatic.net/j/adv-goods.min.js?ce967d90da3c92ad')).done(function () {
                    wb.advGoods.CatalogCardsAdvert.init();
                });
            }());
    


        (function ($) {
            var $container = $(".j-recent-goods-container");
            var action = loadVisitedGoods;

            onScroll($container, '.visited', action);

            $container.on("click", ".j-product-item", function () {
                if ("" != "") {
                    wb.analitics.saveState({
                        l: "",
                        iid: $(this).index()
                    })
                }
            });

            function loadVisitedGoods(container) {
                //console.log('loadVisitedGoods');
                $.post("/visitedgoods", { count: container.attr("data-count") }, function (html) {
                    container.html(html);
                    wb.carousel.renderProductPrices(container, true);
                }, "html");
            }

            function onScroll(container, eventNameSpace, action) {
                var eventName = 'scroll' + eventNameSpace;
                $(window).on(eventName, function () {
                    if (!wb.utils.isElementInViewport(container, true))
                        return;

                    $(window).off(eventNameSpace);
                    action(container);
                }).trigger(eventName);
            }
        })(jQuery);


(function($){
